52b6('bum): cad kyang chos thams cad kyis stong ngo // byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyang zhes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la gan sa shing / bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu
52b7('bum): mngod par rdzogs par 'ad ma par chom gang yang mngon par rdzogs par 'byung chub las sa chos kyi 'a 'phrul yang rnam la// chos gangs 'kho ba 'am kyi 'khor ba 'am/ rab tu 'thar bar dran
52b8('bum): 'amamachim tan de dag ga phyi chos gang yang mthong ngam/ lings su mthong ba gang sangs mchis so // de ci'i srid tu zhen/ da 'di ltar 'khor bar bgyid pa 'am gyi 'thor bar bgyid pa 'am
53a1('bum): tu 'khor bar bgyi ba'i chos de lta bu dmyigs su ma mchis te/ de ni 'di ltar chos thams cad kyang shin tu mngon par ma grub po// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ stong pa nyid ni 'khor bar bgyid pa 'am myi/

53a3('bum): sol// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ de ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa bstand pa dang / rab tu bstand pa dang / bsgrags pa dang // rab tu 'god pa dang / bzhag pa dang / rnam par dbye ba dang / rnam pa
53a4('bum): grol ba dang / smon pa dang / gsal bar bgyid pa dang / pa dag par bstand pa 'di ni zhes rab kyi pha rol dad tu phyin pa ltas de yang sus kyang ma bstand/ sus kyang ma bzla

58b2('bum): 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni byang chub kyi yan lag ni ska rol tu phyidad pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ byang chub kyi yan lag bdun dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro//

58b4('bum): pa dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom lda/ na 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni stong pa nyid kyi pha rold tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka/ 
58b5('bum): stsal pa/ stong pa nyid kyi rnam pa dang rnam par dber pa'i rna/ ma par dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ btso/ ma ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa
58b6('bum): 'di ni mtshan ma mchis pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ zhi ba'i rnam pa myed pa'i phyir ro// gsold pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi
58b7('bum): pha rol tu phyi dad pa 'di ni smond pa myed pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ smonod pa dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gso med pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta
58b8('bum): ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyinang pa 'di ni rnam par tha rang pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ nas par thar pa brgyad dmigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa
59a1('bum): bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'don mthar kyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal dpa// mtha
59a2('bum): tha tha kyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'dug pa dgu dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyi ri pa'o// bcom ldan
59a3('bum): 'das kyis bka' stsal da pa/ sbyin pa dang len pa dang gtong ba dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol
59a4('bum): tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ tshul khrims dang tshul khrims ngan pa dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha
59a5('bum): rol tu phyidad pa 'di ni bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ gnod sems da/ nga bzod pa dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsold pa
59a6('bum): bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ le lo dang brtson 'grus dmyigs su
59a7('bum): byed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ bsam gtan
59a8('bum): dang 'khrug pa dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di ste ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyinid pa 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyining pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bkar
59b1('bum): stsal da ba/ shes rab 'chal pa'i shes rab dmyigs su myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni stabs bcu'i pha rol tu phyind pa 'ang na stobs
59b2('bum): bcu'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ chos thams cad thub pa myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di
59b3('bum): ni myi 'jigs pa bzhi'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyi ye shes zhum pa myed pa'i phyir ro// gsold pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta/ 
59b4('bum): ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di so so yang dag par rig pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka/ da' stsal pa/ rnam pa thas cad mkhyend pa nyid chags pa
59b5('bum): myed pa dang thogs pa myed pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bco ma ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'a daM ni snying rje chen po'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom
59b6('bum): ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sems can thams cad yongs su gtong ba'i phyir ro// gsoyod pa bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma
59b7('bum): 'dres pa bco brgyad kyi pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa'i phyir ro// gsol pa
59b8('bum): bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ brjod pa thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid
60a1('bum): kyi phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni rang byung gi pha rol tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ chos thams cad/ 
60a2('bum): dbang du sbyar ba'i phyir ro// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyidad pa 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi pha rold tu phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ chos thams
60a3('bum): cad rnam pa thams cad du mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir ro// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa stong phrag brgya pa las/ le'u sum bcu pa'o// 
60a4('bum): de nas lha'i dab po brgya byin 'di snyam du gyur te/ zhes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di dag rigs kyi bu dang
60a5('bum): rigs kyi bu mo gang gi rmi lam du grag pa de dag ni sngon gyi rgya la bsnyen bkur byas pa'o// shes rab tu pha rol tu phyind pa 'di sems can gang gi rna lam du grag pa
60a6('bum): de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyirang pa 'di sems cad gang gi rna lam du grag pa de dag ni dge ba'i gshes gnyen kyis yongs su gzung ngo // 
60a7('bum): gang 'dzinid cing 'chang ba dang / zlog cing kun chub par byed pa dang / tshul bzhi du 'di la byed cing gzung ba dang / 'chang ba dang klog pa dang / sum chub par byas nas kyang de bzhin nyid du zhes rab kyis
60a8('bum): rol pa tu phyind pa la nam tan du byed pa lta ci smos te/ rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang gis zhes rab kyi pha rolang tu phyind pa 'di thos nas myi 'jigs myi snga bsgag par myi 'gyur ba de dag das
60b1('bum): sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams la yongs su dris so// yongs su zhus so// rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang gis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
60b2('bum): pa 'di thos nas myi 'jigs kyi sdang skrag par myi 'gyur zhing thos nas 'dzind cing 'chang ba dang / klog cing kun chub par byed pa dang / tshul bzhin du yid la byed pa de dag ni bskal pa bye ba mang por sbyin pa'i
60b3('bum): pha rol tu phyind pa la myod do// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod do// bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod do// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod do// bsam gtan gyi pha ro yod
60b4('bum): tu phyind pa la spyod do// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la myod do snyam pa dang / de nas tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bus padam ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan
60b5('bum): 'das rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang zhes rab kyi rol tu phyind pa zab mo 'di thos nas/ mi 'jigs myi bskrag par myi 'gyur ro// thos nas kyang 'dzind cing 'cha
60b6('bum): ba dang / klog cing kun chub par gyid pa dang / tshul bzhin du yid la bgyid pa de dag ni phyir myi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dang / drad par bzung bar bgyi'o// de ci'i slad du
60b7('bum): zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni zab pa ste/ de ltar sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa dang / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / bzod pa'i rol tu phyind pa
60b8('bum): dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la ma spyad pas ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa zab mo 'di thos
61a1('bum): nas kyang mos par bgyi bar myi nus so// bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa zab mo 'di thos nas/ spang bar sems pa de dag gi/ 
61a2('bum): nini/ sngon gyi mthar yang zhes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa zab mo 'di spangs par gyur to// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo de dag/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa
61a3('bum): zab mo 'di bshad pa'i tshe/ dad pa dang mos ma mchis pa'i slad du ste/ rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo de dag gis sngon gyi mthar yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa'
61a4('bum): sems dpa' chen po rnams dang / nyan thos rnams la bsnyen bkur ma bgyis te/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa la ji ltar spyad par bgyi/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyinid pa la ni ji ltar
61a5('bum): spyad par bgyi/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa ni ji ltar s+ya da par bgyi/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa po ni ji lta/ ra spyad par bgyi/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyinid pa la ni
61a6('bum): ji ltar spyad par bgyi// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa yi ji ltar spyad par bgyi// nang stong pa nyid ni ji ltar sgom par bgyi/ phyi stong pa nyid ni ji ltar sgom par bgyi/ phyi nang stong pa nyid ni ji ltar
61a7('bum): bsgom par bgyi/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ni ji ltar sgom par bgyi/ chen po stong pa nyid ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ don dam pa stong pa nyid ni ji ltar sgom par bgyi/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni ji ltar
61a8('bum): bsgom par bgyi/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ni ji ltar sgom par bgyi// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid ni ji ltar sgom par bgyi/ thog ma dang tha ma myed pa stong pa nyid ni ji ltar bsgom par
61b1('bum): bgyi/ dor ba myed pa stong pa nyid la ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid/ 
61b2('bum): ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ myi dmyigs pa stong pa nyid ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ dngos po myed pa stong pa nyid ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ dngos po
61b3('bum): myed pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ yang dag par spong ba rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnas
61b4('bum): ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ dbang po rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par ba gyi/ stobs rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyid/ byang chub kyi yan lag rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ 'phags pa'i lam yan
61b5('bum): lag brgyad ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ 'phags pa'i bden/ pa rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ bsam gtan rnams/ ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ tshad myed pa rnams ni ji ltar sgom
61b6('bum): par bgyi/ gzugs myed pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ rnam par thard pa brgyad ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi// mthard kyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu ni ji ltar
61b7('bum): bsgom par bgyi// rnam par tha rad pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang mtshan ma myed pa dang smond pa myed pa pasma nad pa myad ma ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ mngon par shes pa rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi// ting nge 'dzin
61b8('bum): rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ mya 'jigs pa rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ so so
62a1('bum): yang dag par rig pa rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ snying rje chen po rnams ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad ni ji ltar bsgom par bgyi// zhes yongs su ma zhus
62a2('bum): yongs su ma dris so// de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis// tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces smras so// btsun pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di ni shin tu zab na/ shes
62a3('bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa zab mo 'di bstand pa'i tshe/ sngon ma spyad pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mos par myi 'gyur ba lta ngo mtshar yang myi che/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa dang / 
62a4('bum): tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol da tu phyind pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / shes rab kyi pha
62a5('bum): rol tu phyind pa dang // nang stong pa nyid dang / phyi stong pa nyid dang / phyi nang stong pa nyid dang / stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dang / tshe/ na po stong pa nyid dang / don dam pa stong pa nyid dang / 'dus byas
62a6('bum): stong pa nyid dang / 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid dang / mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid dang / thog pa dang tha ma myong pa stong pa nyid dang / dor ba myed pa stong pa nyid dang / rang bzhin stong pa nyid dang / chos thas
62a7('bum): cad stong pa nyid dang / rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid dang / myi dmyigs pa stong pa nyid dang / dngos po myed pa stong pa nyid dang / ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid dang / dngos po myed pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid dang // dran
62a8('bum): pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi dang / yang dag par spong ba bzhi dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang / dbang po lnga dang / stobs lnga dang / byang chub kyi yan lag bdun dang / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad
62b1('bum): pa dang / 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams dang / bsam gtan rnams dang / tshad myed pa rnams dang / gzugs myed pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams dang / rnam par tha rad pa brgyad pa dang / mthar da kyis gnas
62b2('bum): pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu dang / rnam par thar da po'i sgo stong pa nyid dang mtshan ma myed pa dang smond pa myed dang / mngon par shes pa rnams dang / ting nge 'dzind rnams dang / gzungs kyi sgo rnams dang
62b3('bum): de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / myi 'jigs pa bzhi dang / so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dang / thams cad shes pa nyid dang / lam gyi rnam
62b4('bum): pa shes pa nyid dang / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid la mos par myi 'gyur ba lta ngo mtshar kyang tsa che// btsun pa sha ra dwa te/ 'i bu shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la phyag 'tshal lo// 
62b5('bum): gang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la phyag 'tshal ba de ni/ tha/ mas cad mkhyend pa'i ye shes la phyag 'tshal ba'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis lha'i dbang po brgya byin la bka' stsal/ 
62b6('bum): de de bzhin no// ke'u shi ka re de bzhin te/ gang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la phyag 'tshal ba de ni/ thams cad zhe nyid kyi ye shes la phyag 'tshal ba'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u sha~M ka 'di las
62b7('bum): byung ba'i sangs rgyas/ bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam pa thams cad mkhye nad pa nyid dan da 'i sa gleb kyi pha rol tu phyind pa brjod do// ke'u shi ka thams cad zhes pa nyid la gnas par
62b8('bum): 'dod pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la gnas par bya'o// lam gyi rnam pa zhes pa nyid kyi ye shes bsgrub par 'dod pa'i/ rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos
63a1('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad spang bar 'dod pa'i// rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos// shes rab kyi pha rol tu
63a2('bum): phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar 'dod pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyidad pa la brtson par bya'o// sems can rnams rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'das
63a3('bum): bu la dgod par 'dod pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// sems can rnams la lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la dkod par 'dod pa'i rigs
63a4('bum): kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// sems can rnams phyir myi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la dgod par 'dod pa'i/ rigs kyi bu 'am rigs
63a5('bum): bu mos/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// sems can rnams dgra bcom pa nyid la dgod par 'dod pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
63a6('bum): pa la brtson par bya'o// sems can rnams rang byang chub la dgod par 'dod pa'i/ rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// sems can rnams bla na myed
63a7('bum): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la dgod par 'dod pa'i/ rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// sems can rnams 'tshang rgya ba nyid la dgod
63a8('bum): par 'dod pa'i// rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// khams kyi phul du 'gyur bar 'dod pa'i rigs kyi bu mos/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
63b1('bum): pa la brtson par bya'o// bdud pham par 'dod pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mos/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// dge slong gi dge 'dun bsdu bar 'dod po'i/ rigs kyi bu 'am/ 
63b2('bum): rigs kyi bu mos/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bya'o// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom
63b3('bum): ldan 'das ji ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la gnas pa lags/ ji ltar na/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / brtson
63b4('bum): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa dang / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / spyi na pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa la gnas pa lags/ bcom
63b5('bum): ldan 'das ji ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpe/ 'chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa/ 'i tshe/ sbyin pa'i pha rold tu phyind pa la brtson par bgyid
63b6('bum): pa lags/ ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bgyid pa lags// ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyirnyed pa la stsa/ 
63b7('bum): pa'i tshe/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bgyid pa lags/ ji ltar na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la yod pa'i tshe/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyidad pa la brtson par bgyid
63b8('bum): pa lags/ ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyird pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par babyed pa lags/ ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod
64a1('bum): pa'i tshe/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtson par bgyid pa lags/ ji ltar na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ nang stong pa nyid la brtson par bgyid pa lags
64a2('bum): ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ phyi stong pa nyid la brtson par bgyid pa lags/ ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ phyi nang stong pa nyid la brtson
64a3('bum): bar bgyid pa lags// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la brtson par bgyid pa lags/ ji ltar na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ chen
64a4('bum): po stong pa nyid la brtson par bgyid pa lags/ ji ltar na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ don dam pa stong pa nyid la brtson par bgyid pa lags/ ji ltar na/ shes
64a5('bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid la brtson par bgyid pa lags/ ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ 'dus ma byas stong

76b5('bum): gtan gyi pha rol tu phyind pa la myi sbyor myi 'byed pa de'i tshe/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyind pa la brtsod par byed do// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyidad pa la myi sbyor myi 'byed de/ gang

76b8('bum): stong pa nyid la kyi spyor gyi 'byed 'i gang gi mi phyi ning stong pa nyid sa kyi spodar gyi ba byed pa dol che/ phyin spong pa nyid la bcin par byed do// gang sa nyid gang pa nyid sa kyi spyor gyi 'byed de/ gang gi se
77a1('bum): slong ba nyis mi spyod myi byed pa das/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la bsod par byed do// na pa gang pa nyid la rgya snar rtswa 'byed de/ gang game che ma stong pa nyid la kyi sbyor kyi 'byed pa de'i tshe
77a2('bum): chen po stong pa nyid la brtsod par byed do// dod dam pa stong pa nyid la myi sbyor myi 'byed de// don dam pa stong pa nyid la myi sbyor myi 'byed pa de'i che/ don das pa stong pa nyid la brtson par byed do// 'dus
77a3('bum): byas stong pa nyid la myi sbyor myi 'byed de/ gang gi tshe 'dus byas stong pa nyid la myi sbyor myi 'byed pa de'i tshe/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid la brtsom par byed do// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la myi sbyor myi 'byed de/ gang

112a3('bum): zhes bya bar myi spyod na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa spyod do// gal te dngos po myed pa stong pa nyid tshad myed do zhes bya bar myi skyon shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyidad pa la spyod do// gal te ngo bo nyid stong

112a6('bum): tshad myed do zhes bya bar myi spyod na zhes rab kyi pha rol tu phyir de ba la myong ngo // kal te rdzu 'phrul ki rkang pa rnams tshad myed do na/ sa bya bar myi spyod na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyird pa la spyod

112b1('bum): myi myod na zhes rab kyi pha rol ba tu phyind pa la spyod do// kal te 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams chang myed do zhes bya bar myi spyod na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la myong ngo // gal te bsam gtan rnams tshad byed
